      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 26th century
       </b>
       . During the period 2501 to 2600 there will be 225
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 83 will be partial, 72 will be annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 64 will be total (one non-central), and 6 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be four, occurring in 8 different years: 2503, 2510, 2521, 2532, 2550, 2568, 2586, and 2597.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
